} function stopMic(){if(G.recognition)G.recognition.stop();} function calcProb(t){var s=70,l=t.toLowerCase(),sp=G.suppliers[G.idx];if(l.indexOf("check")>=0||l.indexOf( "cheques")>=0)s-=10;if(l.indexOf("fee")>=0||l.indexOf("tarifas")>=0)s- =15;if(l.indexOf("busy")>=0||l.indexOf("later")>=0)s- =8;if(l.indexOf("accountant")>=0)s-=10;if(l.indexOf("not interested")>=0)s- =18;if(l.indexOf("yes")>=0)s+=20;if(l.indexOf("interested")>=0)s+=15;s+=Math.rou nd((sp.ach-sp.vcc)/10);return Math.max(5,Math.min(95,s));} function getTag(t){var l=t.toLowerCase();if(l.indexOf("check")>=0||l.indexOf("cheques")>=0)return"Paym ent Method";if(l.indexOf("fee")>=0||l.indexOf("tarifas")>=0)return"Cost";if(l.indexOf("b usy")>=0||l.indexOf("later")>=0)return"Timing";if(l.indexOf("accountant")>=0)retur n"Accounting";if(l.indexOf("not interested")>=0)return"Rejection";return"General";} function getStrat(t,sc){var tag=getTag(t);if(sc>=80)return"Push Next Step";if(tag==="Cost")return"Reframe Value";if(tag==="Payment Method")return"Speed & Simplicity";if(tag==="Timing")return"Keep It Short";if(tag==="Accounting")return"Lower Friction";if(tag==="Rejection")return"Soften & Re-engage";return"Guide Next Step";} function getHeat(s){return s>=80?"Hot":s>=55?"Warm":"Cold";} function getAct(t,sc){var tag=getTag(t);if(sc>=80)return"Ask for setup now";if(tag==="Payment Method")return"Position ACH speed";if(tag==="Cost")return"Reframe: no fees";if(tag==="Timing")return"Short push";if(tag==="Accounting")return"Loop in accounting";if(tag==="Rejection")return"Lower resistance";return"Guide forward";} function getCoach(t,sc){var s=getStrat(t,sc);if(s==="Push Next Step")return"They sound close.
